==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The null check is broken since it will throw a NullPointerException itself. It is likely that you used || instead of && or vice versa.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// should be &&
public class Foo {
    Object buz;
    Object bar(Object list) {
        if (list != null || !list.equals(buz)) {
            return list;
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```
The AST corresponding to this test case(nodes in checker code are better selected from this ast):
ASTCompilationUnit
——ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration (class name = 'Foo')
  ——ASTModifierList
  ——ASTClassOrInterfaceBody
    ——ASTFieldDeclaration
      ——ASTModifierList
      ——ASTClassOrInterfaceType (this is a class type)
      ——ASTVariableDeclarator
        ——ASTVariableDeclaratorId (declared variable name = 'buz')
    ——ASTMethodDeclaration (method name = 'bar')
      ——ASTModifierList
      ——ASTClassOrInterfaceType (method return type = 'Object')
      ——ASTFormalParameters (size = 1)
        ——ASTFormalParameter
          ——ASTModifierList
          ——ASTClassOrInterfaceType (this is a class type)
          ——ASTVariableDeclaratorId (declared variable name = 'list')
      ——ASTBlock
        ——ASTIfStatement
          ——ASTInfixExpression
            ——ASTInfixExpression
              ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'list')
              ——ASTNullLiteral
            ——ASTUnaryExpression
              ——ASTMethodCall (called method name = 'equals')
                ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'list')
                ——ASTArgumentList (size = 1)
                  ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'buz')
          ——ASTBlock
            ——ASTReturnStatement
              ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'list')

Note, when there are consecutive method calls, the last call is at the upper level of the syntax tree.

The checker code framework(you must conform to):
```java

    public rule_name() {
        super(node1_Of_AST_to_visit.class, node2_Of_AST_to_visit.class, ...);

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        return super.visit(node, data);
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpression.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaToken.OROR) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getVariableName().equals("list")) {
                            addViolation(data, expr);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getVariableName().equals("list")) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = infixExpression.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            NodeStream<ASTNullLiteral> nullLiterals = infixExpression.descendants(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = infixExpression.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);

            if (variableAccesses.size() == 2 && nullLiterals.size() == 1 && methodCalls.size() == 1) {
                ASTVariableAccess firstVarAccess = variableAccesses.get(0);
                ASTVariableAccess secondVarAccess = variableAccesses.get(1);
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = methodCalls.get(0);

                if (firstVarAccess.getVariableName().equals(secondVarAccess.getVariableName()) &&
                    methodCall.getMethodName().equals("equals") &&
                    methodCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getVariableName().equals(firstVarAccess.getVariableName())) {
                    addViolation(data, infixExpression);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpression.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getReferencedName().equals("list")) {
                            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = expr.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
                            for (ASTMethodCall methodCall : methodCalls) {
                                if (methodCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                    return super.visit(node, data);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = infixExpr.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.count() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);
                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTUnaryExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTUnaryExpression rightUnary = (ASTUnaryExpression) right;
                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE && rightUnary.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.BANG) {
                        ASTMethodCall methodCall = rightUnary.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                        if (methodCall != null && "equals".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = infixExpr.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCalls.count() == 2) {
                ASTMethodCall firstCall = methodCalls.get(0);
                ASTMethodCall secondCall = methodCalls.get(1);
                if (firstCall.getMethodName().equals("getJane") && secondCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                    ASTVariableAccess firstVarAccess = firstCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    ASTMethodCall nestedCall = secondCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                    if (nestedCall != null && nestedCall.getMethodName().equals("getJane")) {
                        ASTVariableAccess secondVarAccess = nestedCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                        if (firstVarAccess != null && secondVarAccess != null && firstVarAccess.getVariableName().equals(secondVarAccess.getVariableName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = node.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCalls.count() == 2) {
                List<ASTMethodCall> calls = methodCalls.toList();
                if (calls.get(0).getMethodName().equals("getJane") && calls.get(1).getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                    ASTMethodCall getJaneCall = calls.get(0);
                    ASTMethodCall equalsCall = calls.get(1);
                    if (equalsCall.getArguments().size() == 1 && equalsCall.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        ASTStringLiteral stringLiteral = (ASTStringLiteral) equalsCall.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (stringLiteral.getImage().equals("\"\"")) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = infixExpression.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCalls.size() == 2) {
                ASTMethodCall firstCall = methodCalls.get(0);
                ASTMethodCall secondCall = methodCalls.get(1);
                if (firstCall.getMethodName().equals("getJane") && secondCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                    ASTInfixExpression firstInfix = firstCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                    ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = secondCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
                    if (firstInfix != null && unaryExpression != null) {
                        if (firstInfix.getOperator() == JavaToken.OR && unaryExpression.getOperator() == JavaToken.NOT) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = node.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCalls.count() == 2) {
                ASTMethodCall firstCall = methodCalls.get(0);
                ASTMethodCall secondCall = methodCalls.get(1);
                if (firstCall.getMethodName().equals("getJane") && secondCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                    if (firstCall.getArguments().size() == 0 && secondCall.getArguments().size() == 1) {
                        ASTVariableAccess firstAccess = firstCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                        ASTVariableAccess secondAccess = secondCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                        if (firstAccess != null && secondAccess != null && firstAccess.getName().equals(secondAccess.getName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = node.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCalls.count() == 2) {
                ASTMethodCall firstCall = methodCalls.get(0);
                ASTMethodCall secondCall = methodCalls.get(1);
                if (firstCall.getMethodName().equals("getJane") && secondCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                    if (firstCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && secondCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                        ASTVariableAccess firstQualifier = (ASTVariableAccess) firstCall.getQualifier();
                        ASTMethodCall secondQualifier = (ASTMethodCall) secondCall.getQualifier();
                        if (secondQualifier.getMethodName().equals("getJane") && secondQualifier.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                            ASTVariableAccess secondQualifierVar = (ASTVariableAccess) secondQualifier.getQualifier();
                            if (firstQualifier.getName().equals(secondQualifierVar.getName())) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                            NodeStream<ASTNullLiteral> nullLiterals = expr.descendants(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                            if (!nullLiterals.isEmpty()) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                                return super.visit(node, data);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpression.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = expr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = expr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && nullLiteral != null) {
                        ASTMethodCall methodCall = expr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                        if (methodCall != null) {
                            ASTVariableAccess methodCallVariableAccess = methodCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                            if (methodCallVariableAccess != null && methodCallVariableAccess.getImage().equals(variableAccess.getImage())) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> expressions = infixExpression.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (expressions.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = expressions.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = expressions.get(1);
                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && leftInfix.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && leftInfix.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) right;
                        if (methodCall.getMethodName().equals("equals") && methodCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                            ASTVariableAccess qualifier = (ASTVariableAccess) methodCall.getQualifier();
                            ASTVariableAccess leftVariable = (ASTVariableAccess) leftInfix.getLeftOperand();
                            if (qualifier.getVariableName().equals(leftVariable.getVariableName())) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void addViolation(Object data, ASTIfStatement node) {
        addViolation(data, node);
    }
}

```java
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExprs = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExprs) {

                        ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                        if (methodCall != null && methodCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                            ASTVariableAccess methodCallVarAccess = methodCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                            if (methodCallVarAccess != null && methodCallVarAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                            ASTMethodCall methodCall = expr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                            if (methodCall != null && methodCall.getMethodName().equals("equals")) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExprs = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExprs) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && expr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) expr.getLeftOperand();
                    if (varAccess.getVariableName().equals("str")) {
                        ASTInfixExpression nextInfix = infixExpr.getNextSiblingOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                        if (nextInfix != null && nextInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                            ASTMethodCall methodCall = nextInfix.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                            if (methodCall != null && methodCall.getMethodName().equals("length")) {
                                ASTVariableAccess methodVarAccess = methodCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                                if (methodVarAccess != null && methodVarAccess.getVariableName().equals("str")) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExprs = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            boolean hasNullCheck = false;
            boolean hasLengthCheck = false;

            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExprs) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> varAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    NodeStream<ASTNullLiteral> nullLiterals = expr.descendants(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                    if (varAccesses.count() == 1 && nullLiterals.count() == 1) {
                        hasNullCheck = true;
                    }
                } else if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    NodeStream<ASTMethodCall> methodCalls = expr.descendants(ASTMethodCall.class);
                    NodeStream<ASTNumericLiteral> numericLiterals = expr.descendants(ASTNumericLiteral.class);
                    if (methodCalls.count() == 1 && numericLiterals.count() == 1) {
                        hasLengthCheck = true;
                    }
                }
            }

            if (hasNullCheck && hasLengthCheck) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = infixExpression.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression expr : infixExpressions) {
                if (expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.ANDAND) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = expr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getReferencedVariableName().equals("str")) {
                            NodeStream<ASTNullLiteral> nullLiterals = expr.descendants(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                            if (!nullLiterals.isEmpty()) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExprs = infixExpr.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            boolean hasNullCheck = infixExprs.anyMatch(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && expr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && expr.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral);
            boolean hasLengthCheck = infixExprs.anyMatch(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && expr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTMethodCall && ((ASTMethodCall) expr.getLeftOperand()).getMethodName().equals("length") && expr.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNumericLiteral);

            if (hasNullCheck && hasLengthCheck) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.count() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) right;

                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE) {
                        if (isNullCheck(leftInfix) && isBooleanCheck(rightInfix)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                        if (isNullCheck(leftInfix) && isBooleanCheck(rightInfix)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral;
    }

    private boolean isBooleanCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.count() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) right;

                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE) {
                        if (isNullCheck(leftInfix) && isBooleanCheck(rightInfix)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                        if (isNullCheck(leftInfix) && isBooleanCheck(rightInfix)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral;
    }

    private boolean isBooleanCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral;
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression infix : infixExpressions) {
                if (infix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ || infix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = infix.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                        if (varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isPrimitive()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) right;

                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE) {
                        if (isNullCheck(leftInfix) && isBooleanCheck(rightInfix)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                        if (isNullCheck(leftInfix) && isBooleanCheck(rightInfix)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral;
    }

    private boolean isBooleanCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression infixExpr : infixExpressions) {
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQUAL || infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NOTEQUAL) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = infixExpr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    NodeStream<ASTNullLiteral> nullLiterals = infixExpr.descendants(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                    NodeStream<ASTBooleanLiteral> booleanLiterals = infixExpr.descendants(ASTBooleanLiteral.class);

                    if (variableAccesses.count() == 2 && nullLiterals.count() == 1 && booleanLiterals.count() == 1) {
                        addViolation(data, infixExpr);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression infixExpr : infixExpressions) {
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.NE && infixExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && infixExpr.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    ASTInfixExpression nextInfixExpr = infixExpr.getNextSiblingOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                    if (nextInfixExpr != null && (nextInfixExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.NE || nextInfixExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.EQ) && nextInfixExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && nextInfixExpr.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression infixExpr : infixExpressions) {
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE || infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = infixExpr.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    NodeStream<ASTNullLiteral> nullLiterals = infixExpr.descendants(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                    NodeStream<ASTBooleanLiteral> booleanLiterals = infixExpr.descendants(ASTBooleanLiteral.class);

                    if (variableAccesses.count() == 2 && nullLiterals.count() == 1 && booleanLiterals.count() == 1) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression infixExpr : infixExpressions) {
                if (infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.NE && infixExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTVariableAccess leftVar = (ASTVariableAccess) infixExpr.getLeftOperand();
                    if (leftVar.getVarName().equals("boo") && infixExpr.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> nestedInfix = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                        for (ASTInfixExpression nestedExpr : nestedInfix) {
                            if (nestedExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.NE || nestedExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.EQ) {
                                if (nestedExpr.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                                    ASTVariableAccess nestedVar = (ASTVariableAccess) nestedExpr.getLeftOperand();
                                    if (nestedVar.getVarName().equals("boo") && nestedExpr.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTBooleanLiteral) {
                                        addViolation(data, node);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTInfixExpression> infixExpressions = node.descendants(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            for (ASTInfixExpression infix : infixExpressions) {
                if (infix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.NE || infix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = infix.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccesses.count() == 2) {
                        List<ASTVariableAccess> accesses = variableAccesses.toList();
                        if (accesses.get(0).getName().equals(accesses.get(1).getName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && leftInfix.children(ASTNullLiteral.class).nonEmpty()) {
                        ASTVariableAccess leftVar = leftInfix.children(ASTVariableAccess.class).first();
                        ASTVariableAccess rightVar = (ASTVariableAccess) right;

                        if (leftVar.getName().equals(rightVar.getName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && leftInfix.children(ASTNullLiteral.class).nonEmpty()) {
                        ASTVariableAccess rightVar = (ASTVariableAccess) right;
                        if (leftInfix.children(ASTVariableAccess.class).nonEmpty() && leftInfix.children(ASTVariableAccess.class).get(0).getName().equals(rightVar.getName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.count() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && leftInfix.children(ASTNullLiteral.class).nonEmpty()) {
                        ASTVariableAccess rightVar = (ASTVariableAccess) right;
                        ASTVariableAccess leftVar = leftInfix.children(ASTVariableAccess.class).first();
                        if (leftVar != null && leftVar.getName().equals(rightVar.getName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
                    boolean result;
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && ((ASTInfixExpression) left).getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    ASTInfixExpression nullCheck = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (nullCheck.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && nullCheck.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) nullCheck.getLeftOperand();
                        if (right instanceof ASTMethodCall || right instanceof ASTMethodReference || right instanceof ASTFieldAccess || right instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                            if (containsVariableAccess(right, variableAccess.getVariableName())) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean containsVariableAccess(ASTExpression expression, String variableName) {
        if (expression instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            return ((ASTVariableAccess) expression).getVariableName().equals(variableName);
        } else if (expression instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
            return ((ASTMethodCall) expression).getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) ((ASTMethodCall) expression).getQualifier()).getVariableName().equals(variableName);
        } else if (expression instanceof ASTMethodReference) {
            return ((ASTMethodReference) expression).getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) ((ASTMethodReference) expression).getQualifier()).getVariableName().equals(variableName);
        } else if (expression instanceof ASTFieldAccess) {
            return ((ASTFieldAccess) expression).getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) ((ASTFieldAccess) expression).getQualifier()).getVariableName().equals(variableName);
        } else if (expression instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
            return ((ASTConstructorCall) expression).getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) ((ASTConstructorCall) expression).getQualifier()).getVariableName().equals(variableName);
        }
        return false;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.count() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && ((ASTInfixExpression) left).getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (leftInfix.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && leftInfix.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftInfix.getLeftOperand();
                        String varName = varAccess.getName();

                        if (right instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                            ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) right;
                            if (methodCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) methodCall.getQualifier()).getName().equals(varName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        } else if (right instanceof ASTMethodReference) {
                            ASTMethodReference methodRef = (ASTMethodReference) right;
                            if (methodRef.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) methodRef.getQualifier()).getName().equals(varName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        } else if (right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                            ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) right;
                            if (rightInfix.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                                ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) rightInfix.getLeftOperand();
                                if (methodCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) methodCall.getQualifier()).getName().equals(varName)) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            }
                        } else if (right instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                            ASTConstructorCall ctorCall = (ASTConstructorCall) right;
                            if (ctorCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) ctorCall.getQualifier()).getName().equals(varName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && ((ASTInfixExpression) left).getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    ASTInfixExpression nullCheck = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTExpression nullCheckLeft = nullCheck.getLeftOperand();
                    ASTExpression nullCheckRight = nullCheck.getRightOperand();

                    if (nullCheckRight instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        if (containsVariableAccess(right, nullCheckLeft)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean containsVariableAccess(ASTExpression expr, ASTExpression variable) {
        if (expr instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            return ((ASTVariableAccess) expr).getVariableName().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) variable).getVariableName());
        } else if (expr instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
            return containsVariableAccess(((ASTMethodCall) expr).getQualifier(), variable);
        } else if (expr instanceof ASTFieldAccess) {
            return containsVariableAccess(((ASTFieldAccess) expr).getQualifier(), variable);
        } else if (expr instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
            return containsVariableAccess(((ASTConstructorCall) expr).getQualifier(), variable);
        } else if (expr instanceof ASTMethodReference) {
            return containsVariableAccess(((ASTMethodReference) expr).getQualifier(), variable);
        } else if (expr instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            return containsVariableAccess(((ASTInfixExpression) expr).getLeftOperand(), variable) ||
                   containsVariableAccess(((ASTInfixExpression) expr).getRightOperand(), variable);
        }
        return false;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && ((ASTInfixExpression) left).getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    ASTInfixExpression nullCheck = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTExpression nullCheckLeft = nullCheck.getLeftOperand();
                    ASTExpression nullCheckRight = nullCheck.getRightOperand();

                    if (nullCheckRight instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        if (right instanceof ASTMethodCall || right instanceof ASTMethodReference || right instanceof ASTFieldAccess || right instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                            ASTExpression target = null;
                            if (right instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                                target = ((ASTMethodCall) right).getQualifier();
                            } else if (right instanceof ASTMethodReference) {
                                target = ((ASTMethodReference) right).getQualifier();
                            } else if (right instanceof ASTFieldAccess) {
                                target = ((ASTFieldAccess) right).getQualifier();
                            } else if (right instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                                target = ((ASTConstructorCall) right).getQualifier();
                            }

                            if (target != null && target instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) target).getVariableName().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) nullCheckLeft).getVariableName())) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.AND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && ((ASTInfixExpression) left).getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                    ASTInfixExpression nullCheck = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    if (nullCheck.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && nullCheck.getRightOperand() instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                        ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) nullCheck.getLeftOperand();
                        String variableName = variableAccess.getName();

                        if (right instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                            ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) right;
                            if (methodCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) methodCall.getQualifier()).getName().equals(variableName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        } else if (right instanceof ASTMethodReference) {
                            ASTMethodReference methodReference = (ASTMethodReference) right;
                            if (methodReference.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) methodReference.getQualifier()).getName().equals(variableName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        } else if (right instanceof ASTFieldAccess) {
                            ASTFieldAccess fieldAccess = (ASTFieldAccess) right;
                            if (fieldAccess.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) fieldAccess.getQualifier()).getName().equals(variableName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        } else if (right instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                            ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = (ASTConstructorCall) right;
                            if (constructorCall.getQualifier() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) constructorCall.getQualifier()).getName().equals(variableName)) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.OROR) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.count() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) right;

                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                        ASTExpression leftLeft = leftInfix.getLeftOperand();
                        ASTExpression leftRight = leftInfix.getRightOperand();
                        ASTExpression rightLeft = rightInfix.getLeftOperand();
                        ASTExpression rightRight = rightInfix.getRightOperand();

                        if (leftLeft instanceof ASTVariableAccess && leftRight instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                            if (rightLeft instanceof ASTArrayAccess) {
                                ASTArrayAccess arrayAccess = (ASTArrayAccess) rightLeft;
                                if (arrayAccess.getArrayExpression() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                                    ASTVariableAccess arrayVar = (ASTVariableAccess) arrayAccess.getArrayExpression();
                                    if (arrayVar.getVariableName().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) leftLeft).getVariableName())) {
                                        addViolation(data, node);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ANDAND) {
            NodeStream<ASTExpression> operands = node.children(ASTExpression.class);
            if (operands.size() == 2) {
                ASTExpression left = operands.get(0);
                ASTExpression right = operands.get(1);

                if (left instanceof ASTInfixExpression && right instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression leftInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) left;
                    ASTInfixExpression rightInfix = (ASTInfixExpression) right;

                    if (leftInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ && rightInfix.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQ) {
                        ASTExpression leftLeft = leftInfix.getLeftOperand();
                        ASTExpression leftRight = leftInfix.getRightOperand();
                        ASTExpression rightLeft = rightInfix.getLeftOperand();
                        ASTExpression rightRight = rightInfix.getRightOperand();

                        if (leftRight instanceof ASTNullLiteral && rightLeft instanceof ASTArrayAccess) {
                            ASTVariableAccess leftVar = leftLeft.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                            ASTVariableAccess rightVar = rightLeft.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);

                            if (leftVar != null && rightVar != null && leftVar.getName().equals(rightVar.getName())) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
